***провернуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провернуть.html>проверну́ть</a> (19757)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провернуть.html>проверну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">провёртывать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проворачивать.html>провора́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drill a hole in, to perforate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to twist (something) through (something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">esp. meat through a meat grinder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crank</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn with difficulty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quickly do or arrange</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">провороти́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">provorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">low colloquial register</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">except for "to quickly do"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проверте́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">provertétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial register</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>

***проверяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проверяться.html>проверя́ться</a> (18502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проверять.html>проверя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proverjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проверяться.html>проверя́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proverjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прове́риться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do a checkup (usually medical)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to check information about oneself</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проверять.html>проверя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proverjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уравнение.html>уравне́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:легко.html>легко́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проверяться.html>проверя́ться</a></b> подстано́вкой <a href = vnd.unilang:переменный.html>переме́нных</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto uravnénije móžet lexkó <b>proverjátʹsja</b> podstanóvkoj pereménnyx.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">This equation can be easily verified by the variable substitution.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:регулярно.html>регуля́рно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проверяться.html>проверя́ется</a></b> гос-о́рганами.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On reguljárno <b>proverjájetsja</b> gos-órganami.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is being regularly checked by the government.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***провести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провести.html>провести́</a> (658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провести.html>провести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to conduct, to guide, to steer, to take</li>
<li>to lay, to construct, to build, to install <i>a road, a pipe, a wire etc.</i></li>
<li>to carry out, to carry through, to realize, to put into practice, to conduct</li>
<li>to pass over, to run over</li>
<li>to spend, to pass <i>(time)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провести.html>провели́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak vy <b>provelí</b> vrémja?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How was your time?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to book, to register, to enter</li>
<li>to draw <i>a line</i></li>
<li>to cheat, to take in, to trick, to fool</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проветрить.html>прове́трить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provétritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проветривать.html>прове́тривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provétrivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проветрить.html>прове́трить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to air, to ventilate</li></ol>

***провизия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провизия.html>прови́зия</a> (16441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">prowizja</i> or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Provision</i>; ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōvīsiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foresight, diligence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провизия.html>прови́зия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provízija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провизия.html>прови́зии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провизия.html>прови́зии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провизия.html>прови́зий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> provisions, food</li></ol>

***провиниться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провиниться.html>провини́ться</a> (12397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винить.html>вини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провиниться.html>провини́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provinítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be at fault, to commit an offence <i>(in)</i>, to be guilty <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провиниться.html>провини́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provinítʹsja</b> pered kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">do smb wrong; wrong smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провиниться.html>провини́лся</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v čóm on <b>provinílsja</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what's his fault?; what has he done (wrong)?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винить.html>вини́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***провинность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провинность.html>прови́нность</a> (28339)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провиниться.html>провини́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provinítʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to commit an offence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ность</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провинность.html>прови́нность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provínnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провинность.html>прови́нности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провинность.html>прови́нности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провинность.html>прови́нностей</a></b>)

***провинция.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провинция.html>прови́нция</a> (4529)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провинция.html>прови́нция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">províncija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провинция.html>прови́нции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провинция.html>прови́нции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провинция.html>прови́нций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>province (Ancient Rome)</li>
<li>province (administrative region)</li>
<li>area located far from the capital or large urban centers</li></ol>

***провод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провод.html>провод</a> (3449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with stress shift betraying an early derivation.
</p>

<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провод.html>прово́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провод.html>прово́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провод.html>прово́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провод.html>прово́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>leading, conducting, steering</li>
<li>denoting, marking, indicating <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by means of a long line or track</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

***проводивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проводивший.html>проводи́вший</a> (930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводивший.html>проводи́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provodívšij</span>)
</p>

***проводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a> (930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провести.html>провести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spend <i>(time)</i>, to pass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провести.html>провели́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak vy <b>provelí</b> vrémja?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How was your time?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>провожу́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>ве́село</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>provožú</b> vrémja véselo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m spending the time merrily.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electricity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to conduct</li>
<li>to conduct, to lead, to guide</li>
<li>to carry out, to carry through, to realize, to put into practice, to conduct</li>
<li>to put through, to get through</li>
<li>to draw (a line)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay road, to construct</li>
<li>to develop, to pursue</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">bookkeeping</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to enter</li>
<li>to cheat, to deceive</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провожать.html>провожа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to escort, to accompany, to see off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Provodítʹ</b> kovó-libo do dóma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take someone home.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>провожу́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vas <b>provožú</b> do dóma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’ll see you home.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проводник.html>проводни́к</a> (3353)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провод.html>про́вод</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próvod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводник.html>проводни́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provodník</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводник.html>проводника́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводник.html>проводники́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводник.html>проводнико́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводница.html>проводни́ца</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>guide <i>(person)</i></li>
<li>conductor, guard, train attendant <i>(on a train)</i></li>
<li>conductor <i>(physical, electrical)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to escort, to accompany, to see off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провожать.html>провожа́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provožátʹ</b> kovó-libo do dóma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take someone home</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провозгласивший.html>провозгласи́вший</a> (7286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провозгласивший.html>провозгласи́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provozglasívšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провозгласить.html>провозгласи́ть</a> (7286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провозгласить.html>провозгласи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provozglasítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провозглашать.html>провозглаша́ть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to proclaim, to promulgate, to declare, to enunciate (solemnly or officially)</li>
<li>to acclaim <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to declare by acclamations</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
